We're sharing a few of our favorite ways to see the world while ensuring the same right for future generations. Follow the link in our bio for a detailed list of tips and info. What are your eco-friendly travel tips? 🚲 \n1. Begin before you leave: Ready your home for a guilt-free vacation of its own by making sure it’s not bleeding unneeded energy while you’re away.\n2. Bring your reusables: Water and snacks are essential to any traveler’s kit, and shopping for souvenirs is a must, but the potential for waste is great. Whenever you see an opportunity to bypass packaging, take it.\n3. Book a green hotel: Almost every city, from New York to New Orleans, has hotels that are committed to eco-friendly practices, such as saving water and energy and decreasing solid waste.\n4. Bike and walk: To practice the most environmentally friendly travel, walk or bike when possible. Public transportation is a good third resort, and some cities have great eco-friendly options.\n5. Opt for eco-friendly tours: Explore beyond the city to see the nature we’re trying to preserve.\n6. Be informed: Educate yourself on local issues and do your best not to contribute to specific problems of the region, be they cultural or environmental.\n#ecofriendly #gogreen #sustainability #nature #travel #traveltips
